<div class="p-current-events-headlines" role="region" aria-labelledby="Topics&#95;in&#95;the&#95;news"><div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Topics_in_the_news">Topics in the news</h2></div><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1053378754">.mw-parser-output .itn-img{float:right;margin-left:0.5em;margin-top:0.2em}</style><div role="figure" class="itn-img">
<div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; color: inherit; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 128px;">
<span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Mencho_-_2018_Wanted_Poster_(cropped)_(cropped).PNG" class="mw-file-description" title="Nemesio Oseguera Cervantes in 2018"><img alt="Nemesio Oseguera Cervantes in 2018" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d1/Mencho_-_2018_Wanted_Poster_%28cropped%29_%28cropped%29.PNG" decoding="async" width="126" height="155" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="155" data-file-height="191" /></a></span><div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word; text-align: left;">Nemesio Oseguera Cervantes</div></div>
</div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Nemesio_Oseguera_Cervantes" title="Nemesio Oseguera Cervantes">Nemesio Oseguera Cervantes</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, leader of the <a href="/wiki/Jalisco_New_Generation_Cartel" title="Jalisco New Generation Cartel">Jalisco New Generation Cartel</a>, <a href="/wiki/2026_Jalisco_operation" title="2026 Jalisco operation">is killed</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Mexican_Army" title="Mexican Army">Mexican Army</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Jer%C3%AD" title="José Jerí">José Jerí</a> <b><a href="/wiki/Censure_of_Jos%C3%A9_Jer%C3%AD" title="Censure of José Jerí">is removed</a></b> as the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Peru" title="President of Peru">president of Peru</a> by <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_the_Republic_of_Peru" title="Congress of the Republic of Peru">Congress</a>, and replaced by <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Balc%C3%A1zar" title="José María Balcázar">José María Balcázar</a>.</li>
<li>American <a href="/wiki/Civil_and_political_rights" title="Civil and political rights">civil rights</a> leader <b><a href="/wiki/Jesse_Jackson" title="Jesse Jackson">Jesse Jackson</a></b> dies at the <span class="nowrap">age of 84</span>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_Nationalist_Party" title="Bangladesh Nationalist Party">Nationalist Party</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Tarique_Rahman" title="Tarique Rahman">Tarique Rahman</a>, wins <b><a href="/wiki/2026_Bangladeshi_general_election" title="2026 Bangladeshi general election">the Bangladeshi general election</a></b>.</li></ul>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Jalisco_operation" title="2026 Jalisco operation">2026 Jalisco operation</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Nemesio_Oseguera_Cervantes" title="Nemesio Oseguera Cervantes">Nemesio Oseguera "El Mencho" Cervantes</a>, leader of the <a href="/wiki/Jalisco_New_Generation_Cartel" title="Jalisco New Generation Cartel">Jalisco New Generation Cartel</a> (CJNG), and six other gunmen are killed during a security operation carried out by the <a href="/wiki/Mexican_Armed_Forces" title="Mexican Armed Forces">Mexican Armed Forces</a> near <a href="/wiki/Tapalpa" title="Tapalpa">Tapalpa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jalisco" title="Jalisco">Jalisco</a>. In response, CJNG members launched coordinated retaliatory attacks, including road blockades involving burning vehicles and improvised checkpoints across multiple states. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nmas.com.mx/nacional/fuentes-federales-confirman-a-n-la-muerte-de-nemesio-oseguera-cervantes-alias-el-mencho/">(N+)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/jalisco-cartel-drugs-mexico-mencho-new-generation-5014a70bc62a81d74849146c59ba19f8">(AP)</a></li>
<li>At least seven <a href="/wiki/National_Guard_(Mexico)" title="National Guard (Mexico)">Mexican National Guard</a> troops are killed in clashes with CJNG forces in <a href="/wiki/Guanajuato" title="Guanajuato">Guanajuato</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/jalisco-cartel-drugs-mexico-mencho-new-generation-5014a70bc62a81d74849146c59ba19f8">(AP)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/Search_and_rescue" title="Search and rescue">Search and rescue</a> operations begin for three individuals who have been reported missing after a collapse of a <a href="/wiki/Landfill" title="Landfill">landfill</a> in <a href="/wiki/Rodriguez,_Rizal" title="Rodriguez, Rizal">Rodriguez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rizal_(province)" title="Rizal (province)">Rizal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, two days prior. There are other claims that up to 50 people are feared missing from the incident. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.khaleejtimes.com/world/asia/50-feared-missing-after-another-philippines-landfill-collapse">(<i>Kahleej Times</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://mb.com.ph/2026/02/22/3-scavengers-feared-dead-as-landfill-collapses-in-rizal-ocd">(<i>Manila Bulletin</i>)</a></li></ul>

<p><b>Armed conflicts and attacks</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Russo-Ukrainian war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Attacks_in_Russia_during_the_Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Attacks in Russia during the Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Attacks in Russia during the Russo-Ukrainian war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine" title="Armed Forces of Ukraine">Ukrainian forces</a> launch long-range <a href="/wiki/FP-5_Flamingo" title="FP-5 Flamingo">FP-5 Flamingo</a> <a href="/wiki/Cruise_missile" title="Cruise missile">cruise missiles</a>, striking the <a href="/wiki/Votkinsk_Machine_Building_Plant" title="Votkinsk Machine Building Plant">Votkinsk Machine Building Plant</a> in <a href="/wiki/Votkinsk" title="Votkinsk">Votkinsk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Udmurtia" title="Udmurtia">Udmurtia</a>, Russia. Another missile strikes a <a href="/wiki/Natural-gas_processing" title="Natural-gas processing">natural-gas processing</a> plant in <a href="/wiki/Samara_Oblast" title="Samara Oblast">Samara Oblast</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.telegraph.co.uk/world-news/2026/02/21/ukraine-strikes-long-range-missile-factory-russia/">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.dw.com/en/ukraine-strikes-key-industrial-site-in-russia-ukraine-gains/a-76072701">(DW)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eastern_front_of_the_Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Eastern front of the Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Eastern front of the Russo-Ukrainian war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Russian_Ground_Forces" title="Russian Ground Forces">Russian forces</a> capture the village of <a href="/wiki/Karpivka,_Lyman_urban_hromada,_Kramatorsk_Raion,_Donetsk_Oblast" title="Karpivka, Lyman urban hromada, Kramatorsk Raion, Donetsk Oblast">Karpivka</a> in <a href="/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast" title="Donetsk Oblast">Donetsk Oblast</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>, as they attempt to advance towards <a href="/wiki/Lyman,_Ukraine" title="Lyman, Ukraine">Lyman</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.devdiscourse.com/article/law-order/3812823-tensions-escalate-key-developments-in-ukraine-and-russia-conflict?amp">(Devdiscourse)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Insurgency_in_Khyber_Pakhtunkhwa" title="Insurgency in Khyber Pakhtunkhwa">Insurgency in Khyber Pakhtunkhwa</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Afghanistan%E2%80%93Pakistan_clashes_(2024%E2%80%93present)" title="Afghanistan–Pakistan clashes (2024–present)">Afghanistan–Pakistan clashes</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Armed_Forces" title="Pakistan Armed Forces">Pakistan</a> conducts intelligence-based strikes on seven locations along the <a href="/wiki/Durand_Line" title="Durand Line">Durand Line</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Nangarhar_Province" title="Nangarhar Province">Nangarhar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paktika_Province" title="Paktika Province">Paktika provinces</a> of <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> targeting alleged camps of the <a href="/wiki/Pakistani_Taliban" title="Pakistani Taliban">Pakistani Taliban</a> and an affiliate of the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Khorasan_Province" title="Islamic State – Khorasan Province">Islamic State</a>, resulting in dozens of fatalities and injuries. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.ndtv.com/world-news/pakistan-afghanistan-clashes-pak-strikes-terrorist-camps-along-afghan-border-killing-dozens-11119592">(NDTV)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.straitstimes.com/asia/south-asia/pakistan-strikes-militant-camps-in-afghan-border-region-govt">(AFP via <i>The Straits Times</i>)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Army" title="Pakistan Army">soldiers</a> and five militants are killed in a <a href="/wiki/Shootout" title="Shootout">shootout</a> in <a href="/wiki/Bannu" title="Bannu">Bannu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Khyber_Pakhtunkhwa" title="Khyber Pakhtunkhwa">Khyber Pakhtunkhwa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/two-soldiers-five-militants-killed-bannu-pakistan-army-says-2026-02-21/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_conflict_(2024%E2%80%93present)" title="Syrian conflict (2024–present)">Syrian conflict</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State" title="Islamic State">Islamic State</a> claims responsibility for two attacks on security personnel in northern and eastern <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>, in which a soldier and a civilian were killed. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/islamic-state-claims-two-attacks-syrian-army-announces-new-phase-operations-2026-02-21">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Crime_in_Ukraine#Terrorism" title="Crime in Ukraine">Terrorism in Ukraine</a>
<ul><li>A policewoman is killed and at least 15 others are injured, including some seriously, in two explosions at a shop in <a href="/wiki/Lviv" title="Lviv">Lviv</a>, Ukraine. The attacks are being treated as <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.trtworld.com/article/78476603e98b">(TRT World)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Arts and culture</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/76th_Berlin_International_Film_Festival" title="76th Berlin International Film Festival">76th Berlin International Film Festival</a>
<ul><li>At this year's <a href="/wiki/Berlin_International_Film_Festival" title="Berlin International Film Festival">Berlin Film Festival</a>, <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0lker_%C3%87atak" title="İlker Çatak">İlker Çatak</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Yellow_Letters" title="Yellow Letters">Yellow Letters</a></i> wins the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Bear" title="Golden Bear">Golden Bear</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.philstar.com/movies/2026/02/22/2509674/political-drama-yellow-letters-wins-berlins-golden-bear">(AFP via <i>The Philippine Star</i>)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Business and economy</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Tariffs_in_the_second_Trump_administration" title="Tariffs in the second Trump administration">Tariffs in the second Trump administration</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">president</a> <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> raises the global <a href="/wiki/Tariff" title="Tariff">tariff</a> on <a href="/wiki/List_of_imports_of_the_United_States" title="List of imports of the United States">imports</a> from 10% to 15% under <a href="/wiki/Powers_of_the_president_of_the_United_States#Emergency_powers" title="Powers of the president of the United States">emergency powers</a> that permit the measure for up to 150 days after the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">Supreme Court</a> ruled yesterday that <a href="/wiki/International_Emergency_Economic_Powers_Act" title="International Emergency Economic Powers Act">a 1977 law</a> does not authorize the imposition of <a href="/wiki/Liberation_Day_tariffs" title="Liberation Day tariffs">his earlier country-specific tariffs</a>. <a href="/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump" title="Second presidency of Donald Trump">The administration</a> states that the new rate applies broadly, with exemptions for certain sectors and goods covered by existing <a href="/wiki/Trade_agreement" title="Trade agreement">trade agreements</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20260221-trump-hikes-us-global-tariff-rate-to-15">(AFP via France 24)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Disasters and accidents</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2025%E2%80%9326_Australian_bushfire_season" title="2025–26 Australian bushfire season">2025–26 Australian bushfire season</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Victoria_State_Emergency_Service" title="Victoria State Emergency Service">state emergency service</a> of <a href="/wiki/Victoria_(state)" title="Victoria (state)">Victoria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, issues the highest-level <a href="/wiki/Standard_Emergency_Warning_Signal" title="Standard Emergency Warning Signal">emergency evacuation warning</a> for areas surrounding the <a href="/wiki/A1_Mine_Settlement" title="A1 Mine Settlement">A1 Mine Settlement</a> of <a href="/wiki/Gaffneys_Creek" title="Gaffneys Creek">Gaffneys Creek</a>, as an uncontrolled <a href="/wiki/Bushfire" class="mw-redirect" title="Bushfire">bushfire</a> burns the settlement. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/business/environment/residents-australias-victoria-state-urged-evacuate-bushfire-rages-2026-02-21/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libyan_crisis" title="Libyan crisis">Libyan crisis</a>
<ul><li>At least five bodies of <a href="/wiki/Libyan_refugees" title="Libyan refugees">refugees</a> wash ashore near <a href="/wiki/Tripoli,_Libya" title="Tripoli, Libya">Tripoli</a>, <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. Residents also observe a child's body carried back to <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">sea</a> by strong waves, prompting a <a href="/wiki/Libyan_Coast_Guard" title="Libyan Coast Guard">coast guard</a> search operation. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/5-bodies-migrants-washed-ashore-east-libyas-capital-tripoli-police-officer-says-2026-02-21/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li></ul></div></div></div>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Hezbollah%E2%80%93Israel_conflict_(2023%E2%80%93present)" title="Hezbollah–Israel conflict (2023–present)">Hezbollah–Israel conflict</a>
<ul><li>At least 12 people are killed and 33 others are injured in multiple <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> strikes targeting members of <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> across Lebanon. One Hezbollah leader has been reported deceased. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/2/20/one-killed-in-israeli-strike-on-largest-palestinian-refugee-camp-in-lebanon">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://imemc.org/article/12-killed-in-israeli-strikes-across-lebanon/">(IMEMC)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://globalnation.inquirer.net/309804/lebanon-says-8-dead-in-israeli-strikes-on-east-south">(AFP via <i>Philippine Daily Inquirer</i>)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Russo-Ukrainian War</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Crimea_attacks" title="Crimea attacks">Crimea attacks</a>
<ul><li>One person is killed and several buildings are damaged in <a href="/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine" title="Armed Forces of Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> <a href="/wiki/Drone_warfare" title="Drone warfare">drone strikes</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimea</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/one-dead-ukrainian-attack-sevastopol-crimea-governor-says-2026-02-20">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Operation_Southern_Spear" title="Operation Southern Spear">Operation Southern Spear</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/United_States_strikes_on_alleged_drug_traffickers_during_Operation_Southern_Spear" title="United States strikes on alleged drug traffickers during Operation Southern Spear">United States strikes on alleged drug traffickers during Operation Southern Spear</a>
<ul><li>Three people are killed in a strike by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Southern_Command" title="United States Southern Command">United States Southern Command</a> on an alleged <a href="/wiki/Illegal_drug_trade" title="Illegal drug trade">drug trafficking vessel</a> in an area of the eastern <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/2/21/us-military-says-it-attacked-vessel-in-pacific-ocean-killing-three-people">(Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigerian_bandit_conflict" title="Nigerian bandit conflict">Nigerian bandit conflict</a>
<ul><li>At least 50 people are killed and women and children <a href="/wiki/Kidnapping_in_Nigeria" title="Kidnapping in Nigeria">are abducted</a> in overnight attacks by gunmen on a village in <a href="/wiki/Bukkuyum" title="Bukkuyum">Bukkuyum LGA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zamfara_State" title="Zamfara State">Zamfara State</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/attackers-kill-least-50-abduct-women-children-nigerias-zamfara-state-2026-02-20">(Reuters)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://english.news.cn/20260221/2c252d83898c46258632a6a2c308b101/c.html">(Xinhua)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Arts and culture</b>
</p>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Sagrada_Fam%C3%ADlia" title="Sagrada Família">Sagrada Família</a> in <a href="/wiki/Barcelona" title="Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>, reaches its designed height of 172.5 metres (566 feet) after beginning construction in 1882, ahead of the completion of the main building expected later in 2026. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2026/feb/20/barcelona-sagrada-familias-church-central-tower-put-in-place">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>Disasters and accidents</b>
</p>
<ul><li>Seven people are killed, including a pregnant woman, two children are injured and 3,000 are displaced in three <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">landslides</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Provinces_of_the_Philippines" title="Provinces of the Philippines">provinces</a> of <a href="/wiki/Davao_Oriental" title="Davao Oriental">Davao Oriental</a> and <a href="/wiki/Davao_de_Oro" title="Davao de Oro">Davao de Oro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/climate-and-environment/article/torrential-rains-unleash-landslides-that-kill-7-in-southern-philippines">(CTV News)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://newsinfo.inquirer.net/2184520/4-dead-in-mati-landslide">(<i>Philippine Daily Inquirer</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://newsinfo.inquirer.net/2184590/2-children-rescued-in-surigao-del-sur-landslide">(<i>Philippine Daily Inquirer</i>)</a></li>
<li>Seven <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">Chinese</a> <a href="/wiki/Tourism_in_Russia" title="Tourism in Russia">tourists</a> are killed after their van sinks into a frozen-over section of <a href="/wiki/Lake_Baikal" title="Lake Baikal">Lake Baikal</a> on <a href="/wiki/Olkhon_Island" title="Olkhon Island">Olkhon Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Irkutsk_Oblast" title="Irkutsk Oblast">Irkutsk Oblast</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. One person managed to escape the vehicle and reach the surface. An investigation into criminal negligence and safety violations is opened. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.themoscowtimes.com/2026/02/20/chinese-tourists-drown-in-lake-baikal-after-van-falls-through-ice-a92008">(<i>The Moscow Times</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/china/eight-feared-dead-after-bus-with-chinese-tourists-sinks-into-russias-lake-baikal-2026-02-20/">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Seven people are killed and two others are injured in a collision between a van and a truck in <a href="/wiki/Valsad_district" title="Valsad district">Valsad district</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gujarat" title="Gujarat">Gujarat</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.hindustantimes.com/india-news/seven-killed-2-injure-after-van-collides-with-truck-on-hilly-stretch-in-gujarat-101771601377249.html">(<i>Hindustan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Five people are killed, another is injured and power outages are reported during a major snowstorm in <a href="/wiki/Linz" title="Linz">Linz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tyrol_(state)" title="Tyrol (state)">Tyrol</a>, <a href="/wiki/Austria" title="Austria">Austria</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://globalnation.inquirer.net/309811/austria-snowstorm-leaves-five-dead-road-and-power-chaos">(AFP via <i>Philippine Daily Inquirer</i>)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>Health and environment</b>
</p>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Agriculture_(France)" title="Ministry of Agriculture (France)">agriculture ministry</a> authorizes the <a href="/wiki/Culling" title="Culling">culling</a> of around 200 wolves, raising the annual <a href="/wiki/Nuisance_wildlife_management" title="Nuisance wildlife management">removal limit</a> to 21% of the estimated population of over 1,000 animals, with a possible increase to 23%, citing rising <a href="/wiki/Livestock" title="Livestock">livestock</a> losses as wolf numbers expand into agricultural areas and <a href="/wiki/Regions_of_France" title="Regions of France">regions</a> near <a href="/wiki/List_of_communes_in_France_with_over_20,000_inhabitants" title="List of communes in France with over 20,000 inhabitants">major cities</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/france-allows-culling-around-200-wolves-protect-livestock-2026-02-20/">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Gal%C3%A1pagos_National_Park" title="Galápagos National Park">Galápagos National Park</a> releases 158 <a href="/wiki/Captive_breeding" title="Captive breeding">captive-bred</a> juvenile <a href="/wiki/Gal%C3%A1pagos_tortoise" title="Galápagos tortoise">giant tortoises</a> onto <a href="/wiki/Floreana_Island" title="Floreana Island">Floreana Island</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Gal%C3%A1pagos_Islands" title="Galápagos Islands">Galápagos Islands</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a>, marking the species' return more than 180 years after its local extinction in the 1840s. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c9wn1jrzk4go">(BBC News)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>International relations</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iran%E2%80%93United_States_crisis" title="2026 Iran–United States crisis">2026 Iran–United States crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a> relocates some of its approximately 60 <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_Armed_Forces" title="Norwegian Armed Forces">military</a> personnel <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_military_operations_abroad" title="Norwegian military operations abroad">stationed</a> in <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> and other parts of the <a href="/wiki/Middle_East" title="Middle East">Middle East</a> back to Norway and other regional locations, citing security concerns amid heightened tensions between <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/norway-moves-some-its-60-soldiers-middle-east-due-security-situation-2026-02-20/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chile%E2%80%93China_relations" title="Chile–China relations">Chile–China relations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chile%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Chile–United States relations">Chile–United States relations</a>, <a href="/wiki/China%E2%80%93United_States_trade_war" title="China–United States trade war">China–United States trade war</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> revokes the <a href="/wiki/Visa_policy_of_the_United_States" title="Visa policy of the United States">visas</a> of three <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chilean</a> officials, including <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Transport_and_Telecommunications_(Chile)" title="Ministry of Transport and Telecommunications (Chile)">telecommunications minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Juan_Carlos_Mu%C3%B1oz_(politician)" title="Juan Carlos Muñoz (politician)">Juan Carlos Muñoz</a>, after Chile agreed to build a <a href="/wiki/Submarine_cable" title="Submarine cable">submarine cable</a> with <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2026-02-20/us-restricts-visas-for-chile-officials-citing-regional-security">(Bloomberg)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Law and crime</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%932021_Thai_protests" title="2020–2021 Thai protests">2020–2021 Thai protests</a>
<ul><li>A <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> <a href="/wiki/Judiciary_of_Thailand" title="Judiciary of Thailand">court</a> sentences activist lawyer <a href="/wiki/Arnon_Nampa" title="Arnon Nampa">Arnon Nampa</a>, who has been detained since 2023, to an additional two years and eight months in prison for violating the country's <i><a href="/wiki/L%C3%A8se-majest%C3%A9_in_Thailand" title="Lèse-majesté in Thailand">lèse-majesté</a></i> law over remarks made at a 2020 rally. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/thai-court-extends-sentence-lawyer-who-called-monarchy-reform-2026-02-20/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tariffs_in_the_second_Trump_administration" title="Tariffs in the second Trump administration">Tariffs in the second Trump administration</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">Supreme Court</a> rules in <i><a href="/wiki/Learning_Resources_v._Trump" class="mw-redirect" title="Learning Resources v. Trump">Learning Resources v. Trump</a></i> that the <a href="/wiki/International_Emergency_Economic_Powers_Act" title="International Emergency Economic Powers Act">International Emergency Economic Powers Act</a> does not grant the <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> the power to impose trade <a href="/wiki/Tariff" title="Tariff">tariffs</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://edition.cnn.com/2026/02/20/politics/supreme-court-tariffs">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>U.S. president <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> signs <a href="/wiki/Executive_order" title="Executive order">executive orders</a> aimed at implementing tariffs using Section 122 and <a href="/wiki/Section_301_of_the_Trade_Act_of_1974" title="Section 301 of the Trade Act of 1974">Section 301</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Trade_Act_of_1974" title="Trade Act of 1974">Trade Act of 1974</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/china/trump-orders-temporary-10-global-tariff-replace-duties-struck-down-by-us-supreme-2026-02-20/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Politics and elections</b>
</p>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Florida_Legislature" title="Florida Legislature">Florida Legislature</a>, in the United States, passes a measure to <a href="/wiki/List_of_things_named_after_Donald_Trump" title="List of things named after Donald Trump">formally rename</a> <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_International_Airport" title="Palm Beach International Airport">Palm Beach International Airport</a> in <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_County,_Florida" title="Palm Beach County, Florida">Palm Beach County, Florida</a>, as the "President <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald J. Trump</a> International Airport". <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2026/feb/20/palm-beach-airport-renamed-donald-trump">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a>  <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2026-02-20/palm-beach-airport-to-be-renamed-donald-j-trump-international">(Bloomberg)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.telegraph.co.uk/us/news/2026/02/20/florida-airport-renamed-donald-trump/">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>Sports</b>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Winter_Olympics" title="2026 Winter Olympics">2026 Winter Olympics</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Norway_at_the_Olympics" title="Norway at the Olympics">Norway</a> breaks the record for <a href="/wiki/All-time_Olympic_Games_medal_table" title="All-time Olympic Games medal table">most gold medals</a> at a single <a href="/wiki/Winter_Olympics" class="mw-redirect" title="Winter Olympics">Winter Olympics</a> event after skier <a href="/wiki/Johannes_Dale-Skjevdal" title="Johannes Dale-Skjevdal">Johannes Dale-Skjevdal</a> won the country's 17th gold medal in <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a>–<a href="/wiki/Cortina_d%27Ampezzo" title="Cortina d&#39;Ampezzo">Cortina</a>, surpassing their own record of 16 gold medals. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.independent.co.uk/sport/winter-olympics/norway-gold-medals-olympics-dale-skjevdal-biathlon-b2924477.html">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li></ul></li></ul></div></div></div>

</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Terrorism_in_Australia" title="Terrorism in Australia">Terrorism in Australia</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> issues a temporary exclusion order barring one <a href="/wiki/Australian_nationality_law" title="Australian nationality law">citizen</a> held in a <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> <a href="/wiki/Syrian_refugee_camps" title="Syrian refugee camps">detention camp</a> from returning to the country under <a href="/wiki/Anti-terrorism_legislation" title="Anti-terrorism legislation">counter-terrorism legislation</a>, citing the citizen's possible links to <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State" title="Islamic State">Islamic State</a> members. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/australia-ban-citizen-returning-country-under-rarely-used-terror-laws-2026-02-18/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Politics and elections</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Japanese_general_election" title="2026 Japanese general election">2026 Japanese general election</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Sanae_Takaichi" title="Sanae Takaichi">Sanae Takaichi</a> is re-appointed <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister of Japan</a> by the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Representatives_(Japan)" title="House of Representatives (Japan)">House of Representatives</a> after winning the legislative election. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/japan-takaichi-us-china-trump-defense-aa82f8a3b5a7120575072f390f30fb97">(AP)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2028_Philippine_presidential_election" title="2028 Philippine presidential election">2028 Philippine presidential election</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippine</a> <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_Philippines" title="Vice President of the Philippines">vice president</a> <a href="/wiki/Sara_Duterte" title="Sara Duterte">Sara Duterte</a> announces her candidacy in the next <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Philippines" title="President of the Philippines">presidential</a> election. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20260218-philippines-vp-sara-duterte-announces-2028-presidential-run">(AFP via France 24)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/philippine-vice-president-duterte-run-president-2028-elections-2026-02-18/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Censure_of_Jos%C3%A9_Jer%C3%AD" title="Censure of José Jerí">Censure of José Jerí</a>
<ul><li>Following two rounds of voting, <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Balc%C3%A1zar" title="José María Balcázar">José María Balcázar</a> succeeds the removed <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Jer%C3%AD" title="José Jerí">José Jerí</a> as interim <a href="/wiki/President_of_Peru" title="President of Peru">President</a> of <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/peru-president-congress-interim-election-c6f1e2d6c061ea8ba1cb0f4f467609bc">(AP)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Science and technology</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_Gabon" title="Human rights in Gabon">Human rights in Gabon</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Gabon" title="Gabon">Gabon</a> indefinitely <a href="/wiki/Internet_censorship" title="Internet censorship">suspends access</a> to <a href="/wiki/Social_media" title="Social media">social media</a> platforms <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> and <a href="/wiki/TikTok" title="TikTok">TikTok</a> citing concerns they undermine <a href="/wiki/Group_cohesiveness" title="Group cohesiveness">social cohesion</a> and threaten <a href="/wiki/National_security" title="National security">national security</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/sustainability/society-equity/gabon-suspends-social-media-citing-threats-security-stability-2026-02-18/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li></ul></div></div></div>

<p><b>Armed conflicts and attacks</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Russo-Ukrainian war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Eastern_front_of_the_Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Eastern front of the Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Eastern Ukraine campaign</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russian_strikes_against_Ukrainian_infrastructure" title="Russian strikes against Ukrainian infrastructure">Russian strikes against Ukrainian infrastructure</a>
<ul><li>Three <a href="/wiki/Sloviansk_Thermal_Power_Plant" title="Sloviansk Thermal Power Plant">Sloviansk Thermal Power Plant</a> engineers are killed and another is injured in a <a href="/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces" title="Russian Armed Forces">Russian</a> <a href="/wiki/Drone_warfare" title="Drone warfare">drone attack</a> on a vehicle in <a href="/wiki/Mykolaivka,_Donetsk_Oblast" title="Mykolaivka, Donetsk Oblast">Mykolaivka</a>, <a href="/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast" title="Donetsk Oblast">Donetsk Oblast</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://newsukraine.rbc.ua/news/russia-kills-3-ukrainian-power-engineers-1771324972.html">(RBC-Ukraine)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>At least six people are injured and buildings and vehicles are damaged in large-scale Russian strikes on <a href="/wiki/Sumy_Oblast" title="Sumy Oblast">Sumy Oblast</a>, Ukraine. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://newsukraine.rbc.ua/news/russia-massively-strikes-ukraine-s-sumy-region-1771331693.html">(RBC-Ukraine)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis" title="Red Sea crisis">Red Sea crisis</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Naval_co-operation_and_guidance_for_shipping#United_Kingdom_Maritime_Trade_Operations" title="Naval co-operation and guidance for shipping">United Kingdom Maritime Trade Operations</a> says a vessel and a <a href="/wiki/Skiff" title="Skiff">skiff</a> exchanged small-arms fire southwest of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.jpost.com/middle-east/article-886960">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Communal_conflicts_in_Nigeria" title="Communal conflicts in Nigeria">Communal conflicts in Nigeria</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Lakurawa" title="Lakurawa">Lakurawa</a> militants kill 34 people in coordinated shooting attacks on eight villages in <a href="/wiki/Arewa_Dandi" title="Arewa Dandi">Arewa LGA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kebbi_State" title="Kebbi State">Kebbi State</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>. Seven of the villages are destroyed as well as several <a href="/wiki/Cattle_raiding" title="Cattle raiding">cattle are stolen</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/suspected-lakurawa-militants-kill-34-coordinated-attacks-nigerian-villages-2026-02-19/">(Reuters)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.vanguardngr.com/2026/02/terrorist-kill-34-fasting-muslims-in-kebbi-latest-attack/">(Vanguard News)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Business and economy</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Cuban_crisis" title="2026 Cuban crisis">2026 Cuban crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Mining_in_Canada" title="Mining in Canada">Canadian mining</a> firm <a href="/wiki/Sherritt_International" title="Sherritt International">Sherritt International</a> announces that it will suspend operations in <a href="/wiki/Moa,_Cuba" title="Moa, Cuba">Moa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Holgu%C3%ADn_Province" title="Holguín Province">Holguín</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, after planned fuel deliveries were not fulfilled due to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/United_States_embargo_against_Cuba" title="United States embargo against Cuba">blockade</a> affecting oil shipments to the island. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aa.com.tr/en/world/canadian-mining-company-pauses-cuba-operations-due-to-fuel-shortages/3832806">(AA)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Disasters and accidents</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Lake_Tahoe_avalanche" title="2026 Lake Tahoe avalanche">2026 Lake Tahoe avalanche</a>
<ul><li>Eight <a href="/wiki/Backcountry_skiing" title="Backcountry skiing">backcountry skiers</a> are killed, six others are rescued and one is reported missing in an <a href="/wiki/Avalanche" title="Avalanche">avalanche</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Donner_Pass" title="Donner Pass">Donner Pass</a> northwest of <a href="/wiki/Lake_Tahoe" title="Lake Tahoe">Lake Tahoe</a> in <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>, United States. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cbc.ca/news/world/california-avalanche-missing-skiers-survivors-9.7095896">(CBC News)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://abc7.com/post/rescue-underway-missing-skiers-reported-avalanche-castle-peak-area-sierra-nevada-sheriffs-office-says/18612994/">(KABC-TV)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>At least four people are killed and 29 others are injured in a more than 30-vehicle <a href="/wiki/Multiple-vehicle_collision" title="Multiple-vehicle collision">pileup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Pueblo,_Colorado" title="Pueblo, Colorado">Pueblo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://abc7chicago.com/post/pueblo-county-colorado-pileup-crash-today-least-4-killed-25-involving-more-30-vehicles-poor-conditions-tuesday/18612844/">(WLS-TV)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.timesnownews.com/world/us/us-news/i-25-crash-videos-car-pileup-pueblo-colorado-deaths-watch-article-153632041">(Times Now)</a></li>
<li>At least three servicemen are reportedly killed and several others are injured in an explosion at a military commandant's building in <a href="/wiki/Sertolovo" title="Sertolovo">Sertolovo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leningrad_Oblast" title="Leningrad Oblast">Leningrad Oblast</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://news.az/news/explosion-reported-at-military-building-in-russias-leningrad">(News.Az)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/2/17/deadly-explosion-rocks-russian-military-site-near-st-petersburg">(Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>International relations</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_United_States%E2%80%93Iran_crisis" class="mw-redirect" title="2026 United States–Iran crisis">2026 United States–Iran crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> partially closes the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a> for several hours due to <a href="/wiki/Military_exercise" title="Military exercise">military exercises</a> and warns the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> to avoid a military escalation. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.euronews.com/2026/02/17/tehran-threatens-us-and-closes-hormuz-for-drills-amid-nuclear-talks">(Euronews)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/iran-shut-hormuz-strait-few-hours-tuesday-iranian-media-confirms-2026-02-17/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Law and crime</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Killing_of_Quentin_Deranque" title="Killing of Quentin Deranque">Killing of Quentin Deranque</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Police_(France)" title="National Police (France)">police</a> arrest nine people, including an aide to <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(France)" title="National Assembly (France)">legislator</a> <a href="/wiki/Rapha%C3%ABl_Arnault" title="Raphaël Arnault">Raphaël Arnault</a>, in connection with the fatal beating of Quentin Deranque during clashes between <a href="/wiki/Far-left_politics_in_France" title="Far-left politics in France">far-left</a> and <a href="/wiki/Far-right_politics_in_France" title="Far-right politics in France">far-right</a> groups in <a href="/wiki/Lyon" title="Lyon">Lyon</a> last week. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/2/18/france-arrests-nine-over-killing-of-far-right-activist-quentin-deranque">(AFP and Reuters via Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nagorno-Karabakh_conflict" title="Nagorno-Karabakh conflict">Nagorno-Karabakh conflict</a>
<ul><li>An <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijani</a> <a href="/wiki/Judiciary_of_Azerbaijan#Military_Courts" title="Judiciary of Azerbaijan">military court</a> sentences former <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Artsakh" title="Republic of Artsakh">Republic of Artsakh</a> <a href="/wiki/State_Minister_of_Artsakh" title="State Minister of Artsakh">state minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Ruben_Vardanyan_(politician)" title="Ruben Vardanyan (politician)">Ruben Vardanyan</a>, who was arrested in 2023 while leaving <a href="/wiki/Nagorno-Karabakh" title="Nagorno-Karabakh">the region</a> after <a href="/wiki/2023_Azerbaijani_offensive_in_Nagorno-Karabakh" title="2023 Azerbaijani offensive in Nagorno-Karabakh">Azerbaijan regained control</a>, to 20 years in prison for <a href="/wiki/Terrorism_in_Azerbaijan" title="Terrorism in Azerbaijan">terrorism</a>, <a href="/wiki/War_crimes" class="mw-redirect" title="War crimes">war crimes</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity" title="Crimes against humanity">crimes against humanity</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/billionaire-vardanyan-gets-20-years-azerbaijani-prison-state-media-says-2026-02-17/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>A man is killed and eight children are injured in a <a href="/wiki/Crime_in_Mexico" title="Crime in Mexico">shooting</a> at a park in <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_del_Rinc%C3%B3n" title="San Francisco del Rincón">San Francisco del Rincón</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guanajuato" title="Guanajuato">Guanajuato</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gulfnews.com/world/americas/shooting-in-mexican-park-kills-one-wounds-eight-children-official-1.500447922">(AFP via <i>Gulf News</i>)</a></li>
<li>An 18-year-old is arrested after running towards the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Capitol" title="United States Capitol">United States Capitol</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a>, with a loaded <a href="/wiki/Shotgun" title="Shotgun">shotgun</a>, multiple rounds of ammunition and a <a href="/wiki/Bulletproof_vest" title="Bulletproof vest">tactical vest</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/legal/government/man-arrested-after-running-toward-us-capitol-with-loaded-shotgun-say-police-2026-02-17/">(Reuters)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://wjla.com/news/local/police-respond-to-security-concern-at-us-capitol-uscp-lower-west-terrace-politics-democrats-republicans-tourists-man-with-a-gun-rifle-threat-arrest-breaking-president-trump-political-leaders-capitol-building">(WJLA-TV)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>Politics and elections</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Impeachment_of_Jos%C3%A9_Jer%C3%AD" class="mw-redirect" title="Impeachment of José Jerí">Impeachment of José Jerí</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peruvian</a> <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_the_Republic_of_Peru" title="Congress of the Republic of Peru">Congress</a> removes <a href="/wiki/President_of_Peru" title="President of Peru">president</a> <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Jer%C3%AD" title="José Jerí">José Jerí</a> from office following a scandal over undisclosed meetings with <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">Chinese</a> businessmen. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/china/perus-congress-votes-oust-president-jeri-2026-02-17/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Premiership_of_Tarique_Rahman" title="Premiership of Tarique Rahman">Premiership of Tarique Rahman</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_Nationalist_Party" title="Bangladesh Nationalist Party">Bangladesh Nationalist Party</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Tarique_Rahman" title="Tarique Rahman">Tarique Rahman</a> is sworn in as the 11th <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Bangladesh" title="Prime Minister of Bangladesh">prime minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> following the party's victory in <a href="/wiki/2026_Bangladeshi_general_election" title="2026 Bangladeshi general election">the recent election</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2026/feb/17/tarique-rahman-sworn-in-bangladesh-prime-minister">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Science and technology</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse_of_February_17,_2026" title="Solar eclipse of February 17, 2026">Solar eclipse of February 17, 2026</a>
<ul><li>An <a href="/wiki/Annular_solar_eclipse" class="mw-redirect" title="Annular solar eclipse">annular solar eclipse</a> lasting up to 2 minutes and 20 seconds is visible from <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a>, for the first time since <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse_of_April_29,_2014" title="Solar eclipse of April 29, 2014">2014</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Southern_Ocean" title="Southern Ocean">Southern Ocean</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/South_Indian_Ocean" class="mw-redirect" title="South Indian Ocean">South Indian Ocean</a>, and partially observed in <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>.  <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://eclipsewise.com/solar/SEprime/2001-2100/SE2026Feb17Aprime.html">(EclipseWise)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/ring-of-fire-solar-eclipse-february-0d15bb4cd43a8b7eccf6daf7748c5a4a">(AP)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://hub.pl/nauka/news-wyjatkowe-zacmienie-slonca-ziemska-gwiazda-zgasnie-na-ponad-,nId,8066195#ref">(hub.pl)</a></li></ul></li></ul></div></div></div>
